Nothing close these notes arose during interview, stuff interestin motivated enough study it, think that\u2019s enough reason itself, without specific reason. These brief notes. Object Orientated Programmin four aspects: Encapsulat (Hiding informatio Abstractio (Hiding Inheritanc Polymorphi 1. Encapsulat object keeps state private, inside class.
